# User-Choice Audit

Auto-generated by `npm run audit:choices`. Do not hand-edit.

This report joins every tournament-legal card to its parsed effect kind, classifies the kind via [src/engine/_audit/userChoiceAudit.ts](../src/engine/_audit/userChoiceAudit.ts), and reports whether the card's printed user choice is honored by the engine.

**Total rows:** 3250

**Counts:** autoSuspect / high: 0 • autoSuspect / med: 0 • autoSuspect / low: 0 • missingSkip: 0 • unparsedPromptText / high: 25 • unparsedPromptText / med: 97 • unparsedPromptText / low: 9 • prompts: 687 • autoCorrectByRule: 2432

**Status counts:** tested: 3003 • needsFix: 0 • exception: 247 • unparsed: 0

**Status legend:**
- `tested` — classification ∈ {prompts, autoCorrectByRule, missingSkip-with-skip-test} AND a behavior test is registered for the prompt shape.
- `needsFix` — engine auto-resolves a printed user choice; Phase 3/4 will convert this row to a prompt.
- `exception` — listed in `CARD_LEVEL_EXCEPTIONS` with a written rationale.
- `unparsed` — printed text contains prompt-worthy language but the engine has no parsed effect kind.
